<date>1569606011482< /date><rating>5</rating>< text>
I've been here a number of times (lunch and dinner, over the past 3 years or so) and have always had a great experience. The decor isn't much to look at, but all of the food I've had has been extremely fresh and well-prepared. The buffet has a good variety, and all of the fresh veggies are beautiful. And you can't beat the price! Added bonus - I've got fairly serious food allergies, and the way they heat the food, it keeps your stuff on a single space on the griddle. I've been to other Mongolian places where they move the food across the whole griddle, so your stuff gets a lot of contamination from other peoples' plates, but here, your food stays on one section of the griddle until it is done.</text>

<user>105416180571854933460< /user><user_name>Barry Meyer<//user_name><date>1528594831894<//date>< rating>

< review>
I have been using Pacific Beach car wash for many many years as well as the Shell gas station that it is a part of. Now that I no longer need the gas I still go here for the carwash. It is a quick drive through car wash that uses blowers and a big curtain of Chamois to dry your vehicle after your choice of a regular Plus premium or Ultra Deluxe car wash. The Prices range from about 8 to 20 bucks but the feature I use is the car wash Club. For as little as $20 per month for the regular wash you can get unlimited washes each month. They also have an array of vacuums to use 4 coins but included with your car wash club. I must add that I have put all kinds of vehicles successfully through this car wash with no negative effects always a nice clean wash and that the staff is generally very friendly and helpful so it's really a good place to go.<//review>

< Review>
This review is specifically for Tony's detailing service. What a great find! Tony could not have been friendlier, more courteous or more professional. He left my car looking amazing and I could not recommend him enough! To be clear, the car wash is located within the Shell gas station (cheap gas there, btw). You'll see the gas station, then the car wash. Tony is located on the side of the property opposite the gas pumps. If you come in closer to the pumps, it's difficult to see Tony's spot as the large auto carwash is in the way... Just drive around it to find Tony on the other side.</Review>
